			var container = $('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper ul');
		function viewModel_a42_v2_metrostyle_r6(viewModel){
			if( viewModel == 'grid' ){
				container.removeAttr('class');
				$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .viewIcons .list').removeClass('active');
				$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .viewIcons .grid').addClass('active');
			}else{
				container.removeAttr('class');
				container.addClass(viewModel);
				$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .viewIcons .grid').removeClass('active');
				$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .viewIcons .list').addClass('active');
			}
		}

			function changeAmount_a42_v2_metrostyle_r6(difference,id){
				var number = parseInt($('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .number_'+id).text());
				number = number+difference;
				if(number <= 0) return;
				$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .number_'+id).text(number);
				$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .PRODUCT_AMOUNT_'+id).val(number);
			}
			function addToCart_a42_v2_metrostyle_r6(id){
				$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .amountAndAddToCart_'+id).hide();
				$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .addToCart_'+id).addClass('loading').html('<i class="fa fa-spinner fa-spin"></i> SEPETE EKLENYOR...').attr('disabled',true);
				$.post('https://www.horozdemir.com/?p=form_post&obj=a42-v2-metrostyle-r6', $("#a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-form-"+id).serializeArray(), function(data){
					$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .alert_'+id).html(data.MESSAGE).show();
					if (data.SUCCESS == 1){
						$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .alert_'+id).removeClass('alert-danger').addClass('alert-success inline-block');
						$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .amountAndAddToCart_'+id).hide();
						$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .addToCart_'+id).removeClass('loading').html('SEPETE EKLE').attr('disabled',false);
						setTimeout(function(){
							$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .alert_'+id).html('').removeClass('alert-success inline-block').addClass('alert-danger').hide();
							$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .amountAndAddToCart_'+id).show();
						}, 3500);
						cartSmallBoxUpdate();
					} else if (data.ERROR == 1) {
						$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .alert_'+id).removeClass('alert-success inline-block').addClass('alert-danger');
						$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .amountAndAddToCart_'+id).show();
						$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .addToCart_'+id).removeClass('loading').html('SEPETE EKLE').attr('disabled',false);
					}
				}, "json");
			}

		$(document).ready(function(){
			$('.a42-v2-metrostyle-r6-wrapper .viewIcons .grid').addClass('active');
		});

	$.post('?p=form_post&obj=a34-v2-metrostyle-r2', $("#a34-v2-metrostyle-r2-form").serializeArray(), function(data){
		$('.a34-v2-metrostyle-r2-wrapper .alert').html(data.MESSAGE+' <button type="button" class="close" onclick="$(\'.a34-v2-metrostyle-r2-wrapper .alert\').hide();">&times;</button>').show();
		if (data.SUCCESS == 1){
			$('#a34-v2-metrostyle-r2-form')[0].reset();
			$('.a34-v2-metrostyle-r2-wrapper .alert').removeClass('alert-danger').addClass('alert-success');
			setTimeout(function() { $('.a34-v2-metrostyle-r2-wrapper .alert').hide(); }, 3000);
		} else if (data.ERROR == 1) {
			$('.a34-v2-metrostyle-r2-wrapper .alert').removeClass('alert-success').addClass('alert-danger');
		}
		$('#a34-v2-metrostyle-r2-form .newsletter_button').removeClass('loading').html('EKLE').attr('disabled',false);
	}, "json");
};

	function cartSmallBoxUpdate(){
		var valCart = parseInt($("#cartCountTotal").text());

        	url: "?p=form_post&objcart=cartValue",
